 Let's analyze the goal state and feedback:

**Goal State:**

---

### Step-by-Step Analysis:

1. **Variable Name Matching:**  
   Both the goal state and feedback use the same variable name `variable_water_level`. Therefore, we proceed to compare the values.

2. **Value Comparison:**  
   - The goal value is `3`, which is a numerical value.
